<p begin="19454435000t" end="19477791666t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1020">AND I WAS LIKE, "WHAT?"</p>

<p begin="19538519000t" end="19549863666t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1023">I KNOW PEOPLE.</p>
<p begin="19557538000t" end="19567881666t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1024">WHAT ELSE DON'T I LIKE?</p>
<p begin="19568549000t" end="19592573000t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1025">I DON'T LIKE OSTRICHES.<br/>I'M SCARED OF OSTRICHES.</p>

<p begin="19611925666t" end="19636283333t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1027">IT'S A BIG-ASS BIRD<br/>THAT'S THE SAME SIZE AS ME.</p>

<p begin="19655636000t" end="19675656000t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1029">I'M IN NEBRASKA--<br/>DOING A SHOW IN NEBRASKA--</p>

<p begin="19687334333t" end="19703350333t" region="bottomCenter" style="s1" xml:id="subtitle1031">SO I'M ON THE SIDE OF THE ROAD,<br/>I'M PEEING, RIGHT?</p>
